Motivation: 实现多指机器人手灵巧操作，提升机器人对物体在抓取中的灵活控制能力，尤其是滚动操作的能力。

Method: 推导了顺应性准静态多指滚动操作的运动方程，并提出了一个多指滚动操作控制器，利用每个指尖的触觉传感数据（接触位置和力矩），以实现目标物体的期望运动。

Result: 通过仿真验证了接触力学模型，并在实际机器人系统上测试了所提出的控制器，验证了其实用性和有效性。

Conclusion: 多指顺应性触觉机器人可有效实现精确的在手滚动操作，所提控制器具备实验可行性。

Abstract: We investigate in-hand rolling manipulation using a multifingered robot hand, where each finger is compliant and equipped with a tactile fingertip providing contact location and wrench information. We derive the equations of motion for compliant quasistatic in-hand rolling manipulation and formulate a fingertip rolling manipulation controller for multiple fingers to achieve a desired object twist within a grasp. The contact mechanics are demonstrated in simulation and the controller is tested on an experimental robot system.

</details>


### [251] [Perception-Aware Time-Optimal Planning for Quadrotor Waypoint Flight](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04305)
*Chao Qin,Jiaxu Xing,Rudolf Reiter,Angel Romero,Yifan Lin,Hugh H. -T. Liu,Davide Scaramuzza*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对视觉感知约束的四旋翼无人机极限敏捷飞行的时间最优轨迹优化框架，并开发了配套的模型预测跟踪控制器，实现了感知与动态相关的无人机闭环飞行能力，大幅提升了飞行速度与成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有四旋翼轨迹规划常忽略动态、环境几何与视觉状态估算间的耦合，导致在实际闭环飞行中若视觉感知劣化则动作易失败。该论文旨在将感知需求纳入轨迹生成，提升无人机敏捷任务下的可靠性与极限速度。

Method: 提出全新时间最优轨迹优化框架，将非线性动力学、转子极限、气动效应、摄像头视场约束及几何门约束统一建模。引入信息论位置不确定性度量，通过三项感知目标（位置不确定性最小化、时序视场约束、前视对准）耦合进优化。为准确跟踪轨迹，设计了分离横向和进度误差的模型预测型轮廓控制器。

Result: 实验证明系统在现实场景中可实现最高9.8 m/s飞行速度，平均跟踪误差仅0.07 m；在Split-S复杂赛道上飞行的闭环成功率由55%提升至100%。

Conclusion: 本文系统为基于感知约束的时间最优无人机飞行提供了可扩展基准，展示了感知—动态协同下自动飞行的极限能力，对后续相关研究具有基础性指导意义。

Abstract: Agile quadrotor flight pushes the limits of control, actuation, and onboard perception. While time-optimal trajectory planning has been extensively studied, existing approaches typically neglect the tight coupling between vehicle dynamics, environmental geometry, and the visual requirements of onboard state estimation. As a result, trajectories that are dynamically feasible may fail in closed-loop execution due to degraded visual quality. This paper introduces a unified time-optimal trajectory optimization framework for vision-based quadrotors that explicitly incorporates perception constraints alongside full nonlinear dynamics, rotor actuation limits, aerodynamic effects, camera field-of-view constraints, and convex geometric gate representations.
  The proposed formulation solves minimum-time lap trajectories for arbitrary racetracks with diverse gate shapes and orientations, while remaining numerically robust and computationally efficient. We derive an information-theoretic position uncertainty metric to quantify visual state-estimation quality and integrate it into the planner through three perception objectives: position uncertainty minimization, sequential field-of-view constraints, and look-ahead alignment. This enables systematic exploration of the trade-offs between speed and perceptual reliability.
  To accurately track the resulting perception-aware trajectories, we develop a model predictive contouring tracking controller that separates lateral and progress errors. Experiments demonstrate real-world flight speeds up to 9.8 m/s with 0.07 m average tracking error, and closed-loop success rates improved from 55% to 100% on a challenging Split-S course. The proposed system provides a scalable benchmark for studying the fundamental limits of perception-aware, time-optimal autonomous flight.

</details>


### [252] [Gaussian Mixture-Based Inverse Perception Contract for Uncertainty-Aware Robot Navigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04329)
*Bingyao Du,Joonkyung Kim,Yiwei Lyu*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于高斯混合模型的逆感知契约（GM-IPC），用于更精准地描述感知不确定性，并提升机器人在复杂环境中的导航安全性和效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的逆感知契约（IPC）仅用单一椭圆体来描述不确定性，忽略了感知误差的多模态和不规则结构，导致不确定性集过于保守，从而限制机器人导航性能。

Method: 本文提出GM-IPC，将感知不确定性用高斯混合模型生成的多个椭圆体集合描述，能更细致捕捉复杂误差结构。其学习框架联合优化概率包含性、分布匹配和空空间惩罚，以保障预测集合的有效性和紧致性。

Result: 实验显示，GM-IPC提供的不确定性集合能被下游的规划算法利用，实现更高效且安全的实时导航，兼具适应性与安全性。

Conclusion: GM-IPC突破了传统单一椭圆体表征的限制，更好地平衡了安全性与导航进取性，显示出在机器人导航任务中的广阔应用前景。

Abstract: Reliable navigation in cluttered environments requires perception outputs that are not only accurate but also equipped with uncertainty sets suitable for safe control. An inverse perception contract (IPC) provides such a connection by mapping perceptual estimates to sets that contain the ground truth with high confidence. Existing IPC formulations, however, instantiate uncertainty as a single ellipsoidal set and rely on deterministic trust scores to guide robot motion. Such a representation cannot capture the multi-modal and irregular structure of fine-grained perception errors, often resulting in over-conservative sets and degraded navigation performance. In this work, we introduce Gaussian Mixture-based Inverse Perception Contract (GM-IPC), which extends IPC to represent uncertainty with unions of ellipsoidal confidence sets derived from Gaussian mixture models. This design moves beyond deterministic single-set abstractions, enabling fine-grained, multi-modal, and non-convex error structures to be captured with formal guarantees. A learning framework is presented that trains GM-IPC to account for probabilistic inclusion, distribution matching, and empty-space penalties, ensuring both validity and compactness of the predicted sets. We further show that the resulting uncertainty characterizations can be leveraged in downstream planning frameworks for real-time safe navigation, enabling less conservative and more adaptive robot motion while preserving safety in a probabilistic manner.

</details>


### [253] [Tendon Force Modeling for Sim2Real Transfer of Reinforcement Learning Policies for Tendon-Driven Robots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04351)
*Valentin Yuryev,Josie Hughes*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出一种新的力估计模型结合数据驱动与Transformer结构，用于提升肌腱驱动机器人能够更好地将强化学习控制策略从仿真迁移到真实机器人，实现更准确的指尖位姿跟踪。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复杂的肌腱驱动系统虽然能带来灵活性和柔顺性，但其动力学控制极为困难。现有强化学习在仿真中训练出的策略由于‘仿真到现实’差距，往往很难直接应用于真实机器人。本工作旨在攻克该迁移难题。

Method: 设计了一个能获取肌腱在复杂接触场景下真实受力数据的实验平台，利用Transformer等深度学习模型，结合时序历史数据对受力进行高精度建模。然后在基于GPU加速的刚体仿真器中嵌入该模型，实现基于肌腱力驱动的真实模拟以训练强化学习控制器。

Result: 所提方法能将最大电机力3%范围内精确预测肌腱受力，降低了41%的仿真到现实差距，并在机器人手指的指尖跟踪任务实际测试中提升了50%的性能。该方法对不同机器人和执行器具有通用性。

Conclusion: 基于数据驱动的肌腱力建模和集成，极大改进了复杂肌腱驱动机器人强化学习控制策略的迁移与实际性能，为柔性与灵巧机器人的推广提供了新的解决方案。

Abstract: Robots which make use of soft or compliant inter- actions often leverage tendon-driven actuation which enables actuators to be placed more flexibly, and compliance to be maintained. However, controlling complex tendon systems is challenging. Simulation paired with reinforcement learning (RL) could be enable more complex behaviors to be generated. Such methods rely on torque and force-based simulation roll- outs which are limited by the sim-to-real gap, stemming from the actuator and system dynamics, resulting in poor transfer of RL policies onto real robots. To address this, we propose a method to model the tendon forces produced by typical servo motors, focusing specifically on the transfer of RL policies for a tendon driven finger. Our approach extends existing data- driven techniques by leveraging contextual history and a novel data collection test-bench. This test-bench allows us to capture tendon forces undergo contact-rich interactions typical of real- world manipulation. We then utilize our force estimation model in a GPU-accelerated tendon force-driven rigid body simulation to train RL-based controllers. Our transformer-based model is capable of predicting tendon forces within 3% of the maximum motor force and is robot-agnostic. By integrating our learned model into simulation, we reduce the sim-to-real gap for test trajectories by 41%. RL-based controller trained with our model achieves a 50% improvement in fingertip pose tracking tasks on real tendon-driven robotic fingers. This approach is generalizable to different actuators and robot systems, and can enable RL policies to be used widely across tendon systems, advancing capabilities of dexterous manipulators and soft robots.

### [254] [A Soft Robotic Demonstration in the Stratospher](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04352)
*Codrin Tugui,Tirth Thakar,Anatol Gogoj,Alexander White,Ang Leo Li,Alexander Yin,Edward Pomianek,Mihai Duduta*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文介绍了一种新型以紫外光交联的有机硅介电弹性体驱动器，能够在类似太空的极端环境（极端高低温、低气压）下展现出优异的机械和电性能，并成功通过高空气球实验证实其在软体机器人领域的应用前景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 空间及极端环境下的机械设备需要兼具韧性和适应性，传统软体机器人虽适应性强，但对压力和温度极限的适应不足。如何提升弹性体驱动器在极端环境下的稳定性和可靠性，是亟需解决的问题。

Method: 作者提出一种基于trimethyl(methylcyclopentadienyl)platinum(IV)催化剂和紫外光交联机制，使硅烷基与乙烯基发生反应，形成碳-碳键，快速加工成型高性能有机硅弹性体。通过与目前最先进的丙烯酸及有机硅材料对比，实验验证了新材料在-40°C至120°C及近真空环境下的机电性能优势。

Result: 新型有机硅弹性体在极端温度和近真空环境下展现出卓越的电-机械性能。基于该材料制造的夹爪，经高空气球平台集成测试，两次平流层飞行任务都在低温低压下（最高23.6公里、<0.05大气压、-55°C）成功运行。

Conclusion: 该研究不仅证明了紫外交联有机硅弹性体驱动器可用于极端空间环境下的软体机器人，还表明通过进一步优化化学结构和催化剂，可拓展到黏附性及增材制造等更广泛的应用，为后续相关技术发展提供了新思路。

Abstract: Machines designed for operation in Space, as well as other extreme environments, need to be both resilient and adaptable when mission parameters change. Soft robots offer advantages in adaptability, but most lack resilience to the pressure and temperature extremes found as close as the Stratosphere. Dielectric elastomer actuators overcome some of those limitations when built as solid state compliant capacitors capable of converting electrical energy into mechanical work, but the elastomer resilience limits the device's operating window. Here we present a crosslinking mechanism for silicone elastomers under ultraviolet light using trimethyl(methylcyclopentadienyl)platinum(IV) as a catalyst to react hydrosilane to vinyl groups. The formation of carbon-carbon bonds enables fast processing under UV light and exceptional electro-mechanical performance in dielectric elastomer actuators. The material resilience advantage is demonstrated in controlled experiments at -40° and 120° C, as well as near vacuum, in comparison with state-of-the-art acrylic and silicone chemistries. Fully autonomous systems controlling grippers made with the novel silicone were integrated into payloads for high altitude balloon testing. Two stratospheric balloon missions were carried out and demonstrated DEAs as a viable soft robotic technology under space-like conditions (as high as 23.6 km elevation, at <0.05 atm and -55° C). The combinations of chemical building blocks and catalyst can be further expanded to address other challenges for silicones, including adhesion and additive manufacturing.

</details>


### [255] [RoboCasa365: A Large-Scale Simulation Framework for Training and Benchmarking Generalist Robots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04356)
*Soroush Nasiriany,Sepehr Nasiriany,Abhiram Maddukuri,Yuke Zhu*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了RoboCasa365，这是一个面向家庭移动操作任务的大规模通用机器人仿真基准测试集，包含365种日常任务和大量实际及合成演示数据，用于系统性评估和推动通用机器人发展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前机器人学习进展虽快，但缺乏可复现、大规模并系统化的评测基准，难以判断现有方法距离实现通用家庭机器人的距离。为解决此问题，研究者开发了能系统性评估机器人泛化能力和多任务学习能力的新型基准。

Method: RoboCasa365建立在RoboCasa平台基础上，包含2500种不同厨房环境的365项日常任务，采集了超过600小时真人演示及1600小时合成演示数据。可以支持多任务学习、机器人基础模型训练和终身学习等多种研究场景，并对现有方法进行大量实验和分析。

Result: 通过在RoboCasa365上对先进方法的广泛实验，分析了任务多样性、数据集规模和环境变化对机器人泛化能力的影响，总结出影响通用机器人性能的关键因素。

Conclusion: RoboCasa365为家庭机器人的多任务和泛化能力研究提供了系统化评估工具，有助于发现哪些因素最重要，并为推动通用机器人发展策略提供了新的见解。

Abstract: Recent advances in robot learning have accelerated progress toward generalist robots that can perform everyday tasks in human environments. Yet it remains difficult to gauge how close we are to this vision. The field lacks a reproducible, large-scale benchmark for systematic evaluation. To fill this gap, we present RoboCasa365, a comprehensive simulation benchmark for household mobile manipulation. Built on the RoboCasa platform, RoboCasa365 introduces 365 everyday tasks across 2,500 diverse kitchen environments, with over 600 hours of human demonstration data and over 1600 hours of synthetically generated demonstration data -- making it one of the most diverse and large-scale resources for studying generalist policies. RoboCasa365 is designed to support systematic evaluations for different problem settings, including multi-task learning, robot foundation model training, and lifelong learning. We conduct extensive experiments on this benchmark with state-of-the-art methods and analyze the impacts of task diversity, dataset scale, and environment variation on generalization. Our results provide new insights into what factors most strongly affect the performance of generalist robots and inform strategies for future progress in the field.

### [256] [ManipulationNet: An Infrastructure for Benchmarking Real-World Robot Manipulation with Physical Skill Challenges and Embodied Multimodal Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04363)
*Yiting Chen,Kenneth Kimble,Edward H. Adelson,Tamim Asfour,Podshara Chanrungmaneekul,Sachin Chitta,Yash Chitambar,Ziyang Chen,Ken Goldberg,Danica Kragic,Hui Li,Xiang Li,Yunzhu Li,Aaron Prather,Nancy Pollard,Maximo A. Roa-Garzon,Robert Seney,Shuo Sha,Shihefeng Wang,Yu Xiang,Kaifeng Zhang,Yuke Zhu,Kaiyu Hang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出ManipulationNet，作为支持机器人灵巧操作领域科学研究的大规模全球基准测试基础设施。该平台通过标准化硬件与统一软件实现任务复现与结果采集，推动领域标准化发展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前机器人灵巧操作的研究进展碎片化，缺乏统一标准和可重复性高的真实场景基准，阻碍了科学评估和技术对比。为此有必要建立标准化、可扩展的基准测试平台。

Method: ManipulationNet通过标准化硬件套件和统一软件客户端，为机器人操作任务构建可复现的真实世界实验环境，并可进行分布式、多点的性能评测。平台任务分为“物理技能赛道”（低层交互能力）与“具身推理赛道”（高层推理及多模态理解能力），以系统性推动技术发展。

Result: ManipulationNet已实现真实世界任务的标准化配置、实时任务指令下发及统一结果收集，实现了不同研究团队之间可对比的实验，并能够大规模持久运行、组织多元评测任务。

Conclusion: ManipulationNet为机器人灵巧操作领域提供了可持续的基准测试基础设施，有助于系统性衡量科研进展与应用准备度，推动领域标准建立和能力网络化发展。

Abstract: Dexterous manipulation enables robots to purposefully alter the physical world, transforming them from passive observers into active agents in unstructured environments. This capability is the cornerstone of physical artificial intelligence. Despite decades of advances in hardware, perception, control, and learning, progress toward general manipulation systems remains fragmented due to the absence of widely adopted standard benchmarks. The central challenge lies in reconciling the variability of the real world with the reproducibility and authenticity required for rigorous scientific evaluation. To address this, we introduce ManipulationNet, a global infrastructure that hosts real-world benchmark tasks for robotic manipulation. ManipulationNet delivers reproducible task setups through standardized hardware kits, and enables distributed performance evaluation via a unified software client that delivers real-time task instructions and collects benchmarking results. As a persistent and scalable infrastructure, ManipulationNet organizes benchmark tasks into two complementary tracks: 1) the Physical Skills Track, which evaluates low-level physical interaction skills, and 2) the Embodied Reasoning Track, which tests high-level reasoning and multimodal grounding abilities. This design fosters the systematic growth of an interconnected network of real-world abilities and skills, paving the path toward general robotic manipulation. By enabling comparable manipulation research in the real world at scale, this infrastructure establishes a sustainable foundation for measuring long-term scientific progress and identifying capabilities ready for real-world deployment.

</details>
